<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поваляться.html>поваля́ться</a> (23348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поваля́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поваляться.html>поваля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povaljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend some time rolling about or wallowing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поваляться.html>поваля́емся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снегу́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Daváj <b>povaljájemsja</b> v snegú!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Let's <b>roll</b> in the snow!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend some time lying about <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a person — idly or due to illness; of objects — due to being carelessly strewn</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поваля́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***поведать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поведать.html>пове́дать</a> (6166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">powiedzieć</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">powiadać</i>, Czech <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">povědět</i>, Slovak <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">povedať</i>, Serbo-Croatian <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">povijedati</i>, Ukrainian <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">повідати</i>, Belarusian <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">распавядаць</i>, Slovenian <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">povedati</i>, Bulgarian <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">изповя̀дам</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поведать.html>пове́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povédatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пове́дывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tell, to retell, to recount, to say</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассказать.html>рассказа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rasskazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***поведенческий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поведенческий.html>поведе́нческий</a> (31807)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поведение.html>поведе́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povedénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-českij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поведенческий.html>поведе́нческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povedénčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>behavioral</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="2" bgcolor="EEF9FF" rowspan="2" style="vertical-align:center;"><a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a></th>

<th bgcolor="EEF9FF" rowspan="2" align="center" style="vertical-align:center;"> мн. ч.</th>
</tr><tr bgcolor="EEF9FF">

***повезти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезти́</a> (1556)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poveztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to convey, to carry (by vehicle), to deliver, to transport</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be lucky, to have luck, to work out for, to succeed, to be successful (+ dative case)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезло́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne opjátʹ <b>povezló</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'<b>m lucky</b> again. / I <b>got lucky</b> again.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полицейский.html>полице́йские</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выгонять.html>выгоня́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бездомный.html>бездо́мных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> Лиле <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезло́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne vse policéjskije vygonjájut bezdómnyx na moróz, no Lile ne <b>povezló</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Not all policemen chase away the homeless, but Lilya didn't have luck.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Им <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезло́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Im <b>povezló</b> uspétʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They <b>were fortunate (enough)</b> to get there in time. / They <b>were lucky</b> to be there in time.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чрезвычайно.html>чрезвыча́йно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезло́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nam vsem črezvyčájno <b>povezló</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We all <b>were</b> extremely <b>lucky</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***повелевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повелевать.html>повелева́ть</a> (16382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелеть.html>повеле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povelétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелевать.html>повелева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povelevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелеть.html>повеле́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to command, to rule <i>(over)</i></li>
<li>to enjoin, to order, to command
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долг</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повелевать.html>повелева́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">moj dolg <b>povelevájet</b> mne sdélatʹ éto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my duty enjoins me to do it</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:велеть.html>веле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">velétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелеть.html>повеле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povelétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:велеть.html>веле́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелевать.html>повелева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to command, to rule <i>(over)</i></li>
<li>to enjoin, to order, to command</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повелитель.html>повели́тель</a> (8846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелеть.html>повеле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povelétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелитель.html>повели́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povelítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелитель.html>повели́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелитель.html>повели́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелитель.html>повели́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелительница.html>повели́тельница</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sovereign, master (owner of an animal or slave)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повергаемый.html>поверга́емый</a> (25192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повергать.html>поверга́ть</a> (25192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повергнуть.html>пове́ргнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povérgnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повергать.html>поверга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povergátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повергнуть.html>пове́ргнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw down</li>
<li>to plunge <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повергать.html>поверга́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povergátʹ</b> kovó-libo v pečálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to plunge smb into sorrow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повергать.html>поверга́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уныние.html>уны́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povergátʹ</b> kovó-libo v unýnije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to depress smb</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повергнуть.html>пове́ргнуть</a> (16918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ве́ргнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vérgnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повергнуть.html>пове́ргнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povérgnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повергать.html>поверга́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw down</li>
<li>to plunge <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повергнуть.html>пове́ргнуть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povérgnutʹ</b> kovó-libo v pečálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to plunge smb into sorrow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повергнуть.html>пове́ргнуть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уныние.html>уны́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povérgnutʹ</b> kovó-libo v unýnije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to depress smb</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверженный.html>пове́рженный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povéržennyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поверить.html>пове́рить</a> (836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верить.html>ве́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверить.html>пове́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povéritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верить.html>ве́рить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверять.html>поверя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to entrust, to confide, to trust
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверять.html>поверя́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poverjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верить.html>ве́рить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">véritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to check, to verify
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверять.html>поверя́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poverjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to believe, to trust
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верить.html>ве́рить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">véritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to believe in, to have faith in
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верить.html>ве́рить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">véritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:проверить.html>прове́рить</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:испытать.html>испыта́ть</a></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверить.html>пове́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povéritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверка.html>пове́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povérka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверка.html>пове́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверка.html>пове́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поверка.html>пове́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>checking up, check-up, verification
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поверка.html>пове́рку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na povérku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in actual fact, in reality</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поверка.html>пове́рка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povérka</b> vrémeni</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">time signal</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>roll call</li>
<li><i>(of posts, guards)</i> visiting, inspection</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повернуть.html>поверну́ть</a> (1531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повернуть.html>поверну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поворачивать.html>повора́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn, to swing</li>
<li>to turn <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to change direction of one's motion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
